   MACRO SOURCE2 LISTING

     1    /*** TTYPLI - DEMO TTY3270 ****/                                       00000001
     2   -/********************************************************************  00000002
     3    *                                                                   *  00000003
     4    *  TTYPLI - THIS ROUTINE DEMONSTRATES USING TTYRTN OR TTYRTNP       *  00000004
     5    *                                                                   *  00000005
     6    *  NOTE - FOR DYNAMIC CALLS, YOU CAN USE TTYRTN WITH DYNALDA OR     *  00000006
     7    *         TTYRTNP WITH DYNALDP FOR TTY SIMULATION.                  *  00000007
     8    *         FOR STATIC CALLS, YOU MUST USE TTYRTNP.                   *  00000008
     9    *                                                                   *  00000009
    10    ********************************************************************/  00000010
    11   -TTYPLI:PROC OPTIONS(MAIN);                                             00000011
    12        DECLARE                                                            00000012
    13           1  WS_MODULE_BLK,                                               00000013
    14              5  WS_MODULE_NAME1     CHAR(8)   INIT('TTYRTNP'),            00000014
    15              5  WS_MODULE_ADDR      FIXED BIN(31) INIT(0),                00000015
    16              5  WS_CALL_MODE1       CHAR(1)   INIT('K'),                  00000016
    17              5  FILLER              CHAR(3)   INIT((3)' ');               00000017
    18                                                                           00000018
    19        %INCLUDE TTYPARM;                                                  00000019
    20        %INCLUDE AIDCODES;                                                 00000020
    21   1    PUT SKIP LIST('STARTING TTYPLI USING ',WS_MODULE_NAME1);           00000021
    22        PUT SKIP;  /* FORCE STREAM IO BUFFER TO FLUSH. OTHERWISE           00000022
    23                      PREVIOUS PUT WILL NOT SHOW UNTIL AFTER               00000023
    24                      FULL SCREEN OPERATIONS END */                        00000024
    25        TTY_FUNC = TTYFUNC_STRT;                                           00000025
    26        CALL CALL_3270_IO;                                                 00000026
    27                                                                           00000027
    28        TTY_LINE_OUT = 'HELLO WORLD';                                      00000028
    29        TTY_LINE_IN  = '>';                                                00000029
    30        TTY_ERR_MSG  = ' ';                                                00000030
    31        TTY_FUNC = TTYFUNC_PUT;                                            00000031
    32        CALL CALL_3270_IO;                                                 00000032
    33                                                                           00000033
    34        TTY_LINE_OUT = 'TTY3270 PLI HERE';                                 00000034
    35        TTY_LINE_IN  = '>';                                                00000035
    36        TTY_ERR_MSG  = ' ';                                                00000036
    37        TTY_FUNC = TTYFUNC_PUT;                                            00000037
